The dealer shuffles the pack, the player to the dealer's right cuts, and the dealer deals out 2 hands of 11 cards to each player.The remaining cards are left in a stack in the center of the table.\r\n\r\nThe player to the dealer's left has the first turn, and play then proceeds clockwise. A turn begins either by drawing the first card from the stock into the player's hand or by picking up the entire discard pile. Table is a strategy board game for two to four players, in which the players race their four tokens from start to finish according to the rolls of a single die. The game and its variations are popular in many countries and under various names.\r\n\r\nHow to play Ludo Table :\r\nEach player gets to choose tokens of one of the four colors (green, yellow, red or blue). These tokens must make a full turn of the board and then make it to the finish line.
